***pendelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pendelen.html>pendelen</a> (43235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pendeln</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pendulum</i>; ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pendulus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hanging</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pendelen.html>pendelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to commute</li>
<li>(<i>parapsychology/divination; of a pendulum</i>) to oscillate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">commuting</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">forensisme</span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a> (3491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pēnis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tail, <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pes-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penissen.html>penissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penisje.html>penisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span></h4>

***pennant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a> (73605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">penon</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">penoun</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">pynoun</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">penon</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pennon</i>, from <span id="attentionseekingla" class="attentionseeking" lang="la"></span> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">penna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a feather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pennon</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pinion</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pennants</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flag normally used by naval vessels to represent a special condition.
<ol><li>The broad <a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a> flown by <a href = vnd.unilang:commodores.html>commodores</a>.</li>
<li>The church <a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a> indicating religious services are taking place aboard ship.</li>
<li>The commissioning <a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a> flown on ceremonial <a href = vnd.unilang:occasions.html>occasions</a>.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The winning of a competition, represented by a flag.
<dl><dd><i>The New York <a href = vnd.unilang:yankees.html>Yankees</a> have <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a> the American League <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a></b> far more often than any other team.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A rope or strap to which a purchase <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hooked.</li>
<li>A sandstone between coal measures in parts of South Wales</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Not to be confused with <a href = vnd.unilang:pedant.html>pedant</a> (one overly concerned with correctness), nor with pendant (a piece of jewellery).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pennon</span></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:penning.html>penning</a> (5550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">penninc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">pennink</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*panningaz</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penning.html>penning</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penningen.html>penningen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penning.html>penninkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small coin, usually made of silver but <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> also of gold; <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:penny.html>penny</a></span>.</li>
<li>A medal or commemoration coin.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">money</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">cash</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">coin</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penningmeester.html>penningmeester</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">Schimmelpenninck</span></li></ul>

***penoze.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:penoze.html>penoze</a> (68092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פּרנסה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parnose</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life, livelihood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penoze.html>penoze</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> underworld</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:penoze.html>penoze</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***pens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pens.html>pens</a> (23378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pense.html>pense</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">panse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly; tripe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pantex</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly; <a href = vnd.unilang:guts.html>guts</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">paunch</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pens.html>pens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pens.html>pensen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pens.html>pensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pensioen.html>pensioen</a></i>, recorded since 1362, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pension</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">payment, rent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pensio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">payment, rent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pensus</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pendere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to weigh, to pay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***pensioneren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pensioneren.html>pensioneren</a> (125536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pensionner</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pensioneren.html>pensioneren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pension</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take a pension, to pension oneself</li></ol>

***peper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:peper.html>peper</a> (9633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:peper.html>peper</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*pipar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*pepar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:piper.html>piper</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πέπερι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péperi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indo-Aryan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Indo-Aryan languages">Indo-Aryan</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:peper.html>peper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pepers.html>pepers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pepertje.html>pepertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pepper, a tropical major spice.</li>
<li>(short for peperplant) a plant which produces pepper</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:perceel.html>perceel</a></i>, from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">parcheel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">parcelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*particella</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">particula</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:perforatie.html>perforatie</a> (125522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***pergola.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a> (63460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pergula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pergolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A framework in the form of a passageway of <a href = vnd.unilang:columns.html>columns</a> that supports a trelliswork roof; used to support and train climbing plants
<ul><li><b>1919,</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ronald_Firbank" class="extiw" title="w:Ronald Firbank">Ronald Firbank</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valmouth" class="extiw" title="w:Valmouth">Valmouth</a></i>, Duckworth, hardback edition, page 61:
<dl><dd>By the little garden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></b> open to the <a href = vnd.unilang:winds.html>winds</a> some fluttered peacocks <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> blotted nervelessly amid the dripping trees, their heads sunk back beneath their wings: while in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></b> itself, like a fallen storm-cloud, lolled a negress, her levelled, polecat <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> semi-veiled by the nebulous alchemy of the rainbow.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2000</b>, Gordon <a href = vnd.unilang:bock.html>Bock</a>, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=ZhO-43iXnLcCamp;pg=PT56">Pergolas in perspective</a>", <i>Old-House Journal</i>, July/August 2000:
<dl><dd>While both <b>pergolas</b> and arbors are most dramatic cloaked in climbing, flowing plants, only a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></b> will stand naked as a piece of architecture.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Jerri <a href = vnd.unilang:farris.html>Farris</a>, <i>Creating Garden Accents: Step-by-Step Instructions for 22 Projects</i>, Creative Publishing International (2002), →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=u4vF5j9ZXYoCamp;pg=PA98">page 98</a>:
<dl><dd>When I first saw the movie, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:chocolat.html>Chocolat</a></i>, my favorite element wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> the plot or the character development or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> the cinematography. It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the cloth-draped <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pergola.html>pergola</a></b> under which a very special birthday dinner <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> served.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Such a framework employed to provide shade, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> a patio.</li></ol>

***perkament.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:perkament.html>perkament</a> (18555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">percament</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">parchemin</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pergamīna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Περγαμηνός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Pergamēnós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of Pergamun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> named for the Ancient city of <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pergamon" class="extiw" title="w:Pergamon">Pergamon</a></i> (modern Bergama) in Asia Minor, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> invented as an expensive alternative for <a href = vnd.unilang:papyrus.html>papyrus</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perkament.html>perkament</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perkament.html>perkamenten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:perkament.html>perkamentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">parchment</span> (material, uncountable)</li>
<li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">document</span> such as a <span class="Latn" lang="en">certificate</span> scribed on <span class="Latn" lang="en">parchment</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:persconferentie.html>persconferentie</a> (5767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pers.html>pers</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:conferentie.html>conferentie</a></i>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">press conference</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>press conference <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1900]</span></li></ol>

***persoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> (835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">persone</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persōna</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:personen.html>personen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:persoontje.html>persoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>person, individual
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fiction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person, character, personality</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person, hypostasis</li></ol>
